<p><span style="color: #ff0000;">THIS ITEM IS FINAL SALE</span></p>
<p>All of our gauze pieces are made by Mayan artisans in small workshops throughout many different villages in Mexico. We choose not to give our work to huge toxic factories, keeping the longtime handmade, hand-dyed tradition going. Variations in color, shape &amp; style reflect the nature of the gauze itself &amp; the artisanal process taken to create each garment. All embroideries &amp; dye processes are done in small batches by hand, and are meant to be treasured for their imperfections.</p>

Shimmer Scrub: Give skin an undeniable shimmer + glow with this coffee scrub. Boosted with glimmering particles of mica and rejuvenating oils for a gentle, natural exfoliating scrub that buffs skin to a stunning shine without stripping away essential oils or irritating sensitive skin. Made in Australia with no nuts and a vegan-friendly blend. Comes in a waterproof bag.

Magic Shimmer Oil: Dull skin no more with this illuminating dry oil. Hydrates body with a blurring effect for an Insta-worthy filter IRL. Applies so smoothly without any greasy feel, enhanced with a luminous shimmer for skin that stuns. Buildable blend can be mixed with moisturizer for an ultra-hydrating effect. 97% naturally derived, cruelty-free + vegan.

Illuminator: Glow all over with this luminous highlighter. Hydrating blend featuring coconut + jojoba oils with sparkling gold + silver mica for the perfect bit of radiance to brighten up that complexion with a buildable formula that stuns.

Pep up with Frank Body's line of coffee-infused skincare that will leave you soft + smooth from head to toe! Cruelty-free range of scrubs, cleansers and balms made in Australia from naturally derived ingredients with an energizing burst.

**How to Use**  
\- Shimmer Scrub: Apply to wet skin in the shower. Massage scrub over entire body. Leave on for 3 minutes, then rinse. Use 2-3 times per week for best results.  
\- Magic Shimmer Oil: Prep by scrubbing skin and buffing away any dry, flaky areas. Rub an even layer on all areas of exposed skin. Buff in until it’s smooth + absorbed. Wait a few minutes for full absorption before putting on clothes.  
\- Illuminator: Apply to cheekbones, cupid’s bow, brows and nose. May be mixed with moisturizer for extra hydration.
